# Westlake Binder Pivot — Phase 1 Status

**Last updated:** 2026-05-13 (post V2-Step1..Step8-fix: V2 substrate structurally complete and regression-valid at 14/14 PASS. The V2 in-process Java boundary — `WestlakeActivity` / `WestlakeApplication` / thin `WestlakeResources` + arsc parser / `Window`+`PhoneWindow`+`DecorView`+`WindowManagerImpl` stubs — has replaced the V1 `Resources`/`ResourcesImpl` plant chain (M4-PRE12 `AssetManager.mValue`, M4-PRE13 `Configuration.LocaleList`, M4-PRE14 `DisplayAdjustments.mCompatInfo`), the V1 `Activity.attach` try/catch try-fallback (CR23-fix), the abandoned V1 `Window.setTheme` micro-shim hunt (CR25), and the V1 `wireStandaloneActivityResources` per-Activity ShimCompat plumbing. All substituted via `framework_duplicates.txt` classpath-shadow against framework.jar; Activity.attach now a direct 6-arg call in `WestlakeActivityThread.attachActivity` (V2-Step6) with no reflection / no try/catch / no field-set fallback. Substrate: V2 (14/14 regression PASS, noice-discover PHASE G4). V1-path artifacts retained verbatim in the table below as `[SUPERSEDED-V2]` rows for traceability; V1 binder substrate (M1/M2/M3 + the six M4 services M4a/b/c/d/e + M4-power) stands unchanged. **Pre-V2-Step1..Step8-fix:** post-CR26: substrate-level fix for the PF-arch-054 sentinel SIGBUS at the patched `BaseDexClassLoader.toString` JNI lambda — confirmed by audit that NO code in `art-latest/` writes the `kPFCutStaleNativeEntry` sentinel into `JNINativeInterface::NewStringUTF` (all 48 references in art-latest are READERS that detect-and-repair stale entries; the 28 MB dalvikvm binary contains 0 literal copies of the sentinel byte pattern; the static `gJniNativeInterface` table in .rodata is well-formed). On the failing call path `env->functions` is corrupted — pointing at memory outside the static table whose offset 1336 happens to be the sentinel (or random garbage; CR13 §2.4 once observed ASCII `"c method "` at the same slot). **PF-arch-055 fix**: rewrite the patched lambda body in `art-latest/patches/runtime/runtime.cc:2745-2820` to use `mirror::String::AllocFromModifiedUtf8` + `JNIEnvExt::AddLocalReference` — both direct C++ symbol calls that don't traverse the JNINativeInterface vtable. Disassembly verification: new function body at `0x6744b4` is `0xf8` bytes (was `0x24`) and contains no `[x8, #1336]` slot read; the fault site is unreachable. **Verification with CR24 workaround temporarily reverted (`+ appPCL` restored to force String.valueOf via patched lambda)**: noice-discover.sh exit 0, PHASE A-G4 all reached, 0 SIGBUS in log. **Full regression with CR24 workaround restored**: 14/14 PASS. dalvikvm rebuilt (md5 `c4ab142009d534fdf2b1b5b68fc2575c`); CR15's widened guard remains in source as dead-code documentation; CR24's identityHashCode workaround retained verbatim as belt-and-suspenders with one updated comment block. Underlying mystery WHY `env->functions` gets corrupted remains open for a future CR (CR13 §6.3 suggests `hw watchpoint --write 0xfad8f8`) but no longer blocks discovery progress. Pre-CR26: post-CR27: refactored `NoiceDiscoverWrapper.java` from 1195 LOC monolith into manifest-driven `DiscoverWrapperBase` (NEW, 1140 LOC) + slim `NoiceDiscoverWrapper.java` (60 LOC) + NEW `McdDiscoverWrapper.java` (70 LOC) + per-app `.properties` manifests (noice + mcd, 73 lines total) — net +75 LOC across test/ Java for the manifest loader / Printer interface scaffolding. Per codex review #2 Tier 3: "should become manifest-driven before it is reused for a second app". Acceptance: `noice-discover.sh` still reaches **PHASE G4** (same as post-CR24); new `mcd-discover.sh` reaches **PHASE G3** on first attempt — PHASE A 7/70 services / PHASE B **7/7 McD classes loadable** (McDMarketApplication, SplashActivity, etc.) / PHASE C `new McDMarketApplication()` clean / PHASE D `attachBaseContext` OK / PHASE G2 SplashActivity instantiated / PHASE G3 Activity.attach throws (the next McD discovery boundary, separate fix). No per-app branches in the base class. CR24 PF-arch-054 workaround preserved verbatim. Pre-CR27: post-CR24: PHASE B "hang" on `noice-discover.sh` diagnosed as the **recurring PF-arch-054 SIGBUS** at PC=`0xfffffffffffffb17` from CR13 — what looked like a >13-minute Java infinite loop is actually ART's `HandleUnexpectedSignalLinux → UContext::Dump → vsnprintf → write` signal-handler dumper grinding through stack walk + memory-map dump (simpleperf confirmed ~70% CPU in kernel `do_el0_ia_bp_hardening / __handle_speculative_fault / handle_pte_fault` while the dumper runs); the SIGBUS itself fires inside the patched `loader_to_string` JNI trampoline when `NoiceDiscoverWrapper.phaseB_classLoad:329` does `String.valueOf(noicePCL)` via `+ noicePCL` concatenation. Fix applied per CR13's fix path #1: replaced the `+ noicePCL` log concatenation with `System.identityHashCode(noicePCL) + getClass().getName()`, neither of which invokes the patched JNI `toString`. NoiceDiscoverWrapper.dex rebuilt (32 KB) + pushed. `noice-discover.sh` now reaches **PHASE G4** (the pre-reboot peak — MainActivity.onCreate body executing with a fresh `Configuration.setTo(null)` NPE that is the M4-PRE15-or-later discovery boundary). **Full regression suite: 14/14 PASS** (previously 13/13 PASS + 1 noice FAIL). Underlying art-latest substrate bug (NewStringUTF function-table slot getting overwritten with `kPFCutStaleNativeEntry` before the trampoline branches) remains open — CR24 sidesteps; does not fix. Pre-CR24: post-CR19 — `WestlakePackageManagerStub` (M4-PRE5's LOCAL `Context.getPackageManager()` impl) fail-loud conversion per codex review #2 Tier 2 finding — 168 non-Tier-1 silent stubs (`return null/false/0/empty`) converted to `throw ServiceMethodMissing.fail("packageManager", "<methodName>")` mirroring CR2's pattern for the binder-backed M4 services; 11 Tier-1 methods (`getServiceInfo`/`getActivityInfo`/`getApplicationInfo`/`getPackageInfo`/`hasSystemFeature`×2/`resolveActivity`/`resolveService`/`queryIntentActivities`/`getInstalledPackages`/`checkPermission`) preserved unchanged; aosp-shim.dex 1,380,980 → 1,383,652 bytes (+2,672 B / +0.19%); zero `WestlakeServiceMethodMissing` markers fired in 5 quick-regression runs (failures rotated across `sm_smoke`/`HelloBinder`/`SystemServiceRouteTest`/`InputMethodServiceTest`/`NotificationServiceTest`/`WindowServiceTest` — sm_smoke and HelloBinder don't even load the shim DEX, proving the flakiness is infra not CR19); noice-discover PHASE B SIGBUS (CR15 / PF-arch-054) still the unchanged high-water mark since CR19 targets methods downstream of where the SIGBUS hits. Pre-CR19: post-CR17 — M4d/M4e PermissionEnforcer bypass moved into production code; M4d/M4e services proven self-sufficient. Pre-CR17: post-CR15 — PF-arch-054 widen-the-guard applied to `loader_to_string` JNI lambda at `art-latest/patches/runtime/runtime.cc:2750-2767` — rejects both `nullptr` and `kPFCutStaleNativeEntry` (`0xfffffffffffffb17`); dalvikvm rebuilt clean (md5 `7546afc6...` → `807cf339...`, Δ=-72 B); deployed to phone `cfb7c9e3`; HelloBinder still PASS; **but `noice-discover.sh` STILL SIGBUSes at the same sentinel PC at PHASE B** — disproving CR13's proximate-cause hypothesis. **Open mystery still open**: WHO writes the sentinel into `JNINativeInterface::NewStringUTF` slot — CR17-class follow-up needed (hw watchpoint on `0xfad8f8`). Pre-CR15: post-CR16 — WestlakeLauncher.java CR14-deferred sections migrated (S3/S12/S15/S16); 22,983 → 12,668 LOC (-44.9%) vs original.)
**Read first (V2 authoritative):** `BINDER_PIVOT_DESIGN_V2.md` (CR28-architect 2026-05-13; the operational design for the in-process Java boundary; supersedes V1 §3.2/§3.3/§3.4/§3.5), `MIGRATION_FROM_V1.md` (V2 implementation deltas, file-by-file keep/touch/delete), `V2_STEP6_DIFF_SPEC.md` (V2-Step6 attachActivity rewire), `V2_STEP7_PLANT_RESIDUE_AUDIT.md` (V2-Step7 audit + the one deletion that landed), `V2_STEP8_FIX_CHARSET_NPE.md` (V2-Step8-fix bisection + dalvikvm sync fix).

This document is the canonical snapshot of where Phase 1 is. It is updated
after every milestone; agents starting work should read it first. For the
narrative blow-by-blow per milestone, see `M4_DISCOVERY.md` (which carries the
section-by-section discovery transcripts).

## 1. Headline

All 2026-05-12 dates below mean the work landed on the same calendar day
(Phase 1 was sprinted over a single-day push following the
2026-05-12 binder-pivot decision). "Owner" is the swarm role / agent
role, not a person. "Result-summary" is one sentence; full detail lives
in the M4_DISCOVERY.md §N pointer under Files-touched.

### 1.3 Discovery + Tier-1 service work (M4 + M4-PRE + CR iterations) — 2026-05-12

The M4-PRE* sub-milestones surfaced through W2-discover's subtraction
harness; each is a real-app-driven discovery of a missing plumbing piece
that blocks `Activity.attach` from completing. Each row's last column
points to the canonical M4_DISCOVERY.md section (post-DOC1 renumber).

| Milestone | Status | Date | Owner | Result-summary | Files-touched (key) | M4_DISCOVERY § |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| M6-Step6 — Apply CR35 §7 AIDL-drift mitigation: A15 descriptor + transaction-code translation shim | done (build clean 2026-05-13; m6step5-smoke 8/8 PASS preserved; CR35 §7 §D-B descriptor tolerance + §D-C A15 AIDL code-table both wired; T1-D/T1-E already addressed in earlier Steps per CR35 §10; §T2-A/B/§T3-A and §D-A explicit-strace audit deferred to M7-Step2 as CR35 recommends) | 2026-05-13 | Builder (this work) | CR35 §7 surfaced 16 implementor TODO items split across Tier-1 polish (§T1-A..E), Tier-2 fail-soft (§T2-A..C), Tier-3 fail-loud (§T3-A), A15 drift mitigation (§D-A..D), and wire-format edge cases (§E-A..C). M6-Step6 triaged the list per the task brief: items that touch THIS daemon (`aosp-surface-daemon-port/native/`) at the descriptor/transaction-dispatch boundary land now; items that require real-app traffic audit (§D-A strace), Tier-2/3 promotions risking fall-through-mask hides, or libgui-AIDL regen (§T1-A's ~600 LOC Parcelable path) defer to M7-Step2 informed by real on-wire codes. **Items applied this CR (3)**: **§7 §D-B** — descriptor-tolerant header probe at `WestlakeSurfaceComposer::onTransact` and `WestlakeSurfaceComposerClient::onTransact`. The strict `CHECK_INTERFACE(ISurfaceComposer, data, reply)` (which reduces to `Parcel::enforceInterface` → strict-string-compare against `this->getInterfaceDescriptor()`, rejecting any peer that writes a different descriptor with `PERMISSION_DENIED`) is replaced with a new helper `checkSurfaceComposerInterface(data, *outIsA15)` that (a) consumes the same Parcel header bytes (StrictModePolicy, WorkSource, kHeader, descriptor String16) so handlers see the same post-header read position, (b) accepts EITHER the AOSP-11 form `"android.ui.ISurfaceComposer"` (the IMPLEMENT_META_INTERFACE value our surface_smoke peer writes) OR the A15 AIDL form `"android.ISurfaceComposer"` (per CR35 §6.6's `nm -D libgui.so` evidence showing `_ZN7android16ISurfaceComposer10descriptorE` with no `ui::` segment), and (c) sets `*outIsA15` so the dispatcher can route to the matching code-table. Pattern is symmetric with CR11's libbinder kHeader receive-tolerance (`Parcel.cpp` §1106-1117 §enforceInterface) — receive widely, send canonically. Same widening applied to `WestlakeSurfaceComposerClient::onTransact` for `"android.ui.ISurfaceComposerClient"` vs `"android.gui.ISurfaceComposerClient"` (per CR35 §6.3 + §6.6 namespace drift). **§7 §D-C** — `WestlakeSurfaceComposer::dispatchA15Code(code, data, reply)` new method invoked when the descriptor probe observed the A15 form. Maps ~17 A15 AIDL codes (carryover-equivalent or rename-equivalent of AOSP-11 enums) to the existing AOSP-11 handlers: e.g. `A15_BOOT_FINISHED` → `onBootFinished`; `A15_CREATE_VIRTUAL_DISPLAY` (A15 rename of `CREATE_DISPLAY`) → `onCreateDisplay`; `A15_GET_STATIC_DISPLAY_INFO` + `A15_GET_DYNAMIC_DISPLAY_INFO_FROM_TOKEN` + `A15_GET_DYNAMIC_DISPLAY_INFO_FROM_ID` (the A15 split of `GET_DISPLAY_INFO` per CR35 §6.2) → `onGetDisplayInfo` (the 96-byte zeroed envelope deserializes safely as either struct shape); `A15_NOTIFY_POWER_BOOST` (A14+ rename of `NOTIFY_POWER_HINT`) acked; capture codes return `BAD_VALUE` per CR35 §2 Tier-3 notes. **Carries CRITICAL CAVEAT in-code** (cross-ref to §D-A strace audit pending): the AIDL code numbers in the new `WestlakeSurfaceComposer::A15AidlCode` enum are derived from alphabetical-ordering of CR35 §6.2's 75 method names — single point of fix when M7-Step2 strace confirms or refutes any code. Phase-1 graceful-degradation contract is preserved: codes not in the table log + ack with empty reply (never crash, never `PERMISSION_DENIED`). **§7 §D-D** (partial) — fail-loud-via-log for net-new A15 methods is achieved via the explicit `[wlk-sf] A15 code=%u not in CR35 §D-C translation table` log line in `dispatchA15Code`'s default branch, so M7-Step2's first strace will surface every actual on-wire code that isn't yet mapped. Full `ALOGE + return INVALID_OPERATION` per CR35 §T3-A is deferred per CR35's own guidance ("Do AFTER one full noice/McD discovery run"). **Items deferred to M7-Step2 / future (8 substantive)**: §T1-A (worst-case-envelope → explicit Parcelable for DisplayInfo/DisplayConfig/DisplayState, ~80 LOC) — current envelope works for AOSP-11 smoke, real-app fields are zero-tolerant; revisit when host APK reads non-zero fields. §T2-A (19 ISurfaceComposer Tier-2 explicit handlers, ~250 LOC) — current ack-only-with-NO_ERROR+empty-reply path is safe for Phase-1, explicit handlers are an observability improvement, not a correctness fix; defer until §D-A strace shows which Tier-2 codes real apps actually hit. §T2-B (6 IGraphicBufferProducer Tier-2 handlers, ~80 LOC) — same rationale; M6-Step3's IGBP code already covers Tier-1 hot path. §T3-A (18 ISC + 8 IGBP Tier-3 fail-loud, ~100 LOC) — CR35 itself recommends doing this AFTER one noice/McD strace run. §D-A (M7-Step2 strace + reconcile against §2/§3/§4/§5 tables) — that's M7-Step2's job. §D-D residual (~50 LOC ALOGE stubs for 25 net-new A15 methods + 2 IDisplayEventConnection + 2 ISurfaceComposerClient) — current log-line gives the same observability without static enumeration; once §D-A strace audit lands, the named stubs (using `WestlakeServiceMethodMissing.fail()` per CR17 pattern) become a 1-CR refactor. **Items already landed in earlier M6 Steps (5 — no new work)**: §T1-B (IGraphicBufferProducer Tier-1 — M6-Step3 done), §T1-C (IDisplayEventConnection Tier-1 — M6-Step4 done + Step-5 vsync), §T1-D (real BnDisplayEventConnection — M6-Step5 done), §T1-E (real BnGraphicBufferProducer from CREATE_SURFACE — M6-Step3 done), §E-A (IGBP typo preservation — M6-Step3 honored), §E-B (SafeInterface reply ordering — M6-Step2 ISCC honored), §E-C (no RESERVED slots — N/A). **Smoke regression result**: `m6step5-smoke.sh` 8/8 PASS on phone `cfb7c9e3` — A (CREATE_CONNECTION), B (CREATE_SURFACE), C (DEQUEUE/QUEUE_BUFFER × 2), D (CREATE_DISPLAY_EVENT_CONNECTION + vsync sub), E (regression: GET_PHYSICAL_DISPLAY_IDS + GET_PHYSICAL_DISPLAY_TOKEN + GET_DISPLAY_STATS), F (IGBP roundtrip), G (DLST pipe), H (3-vsync-event + spacing within 8-35ms tolerance for ~60Hz). Daemon log shows clean construction + per-handler trace; descriptor probe consumes the AOSP-11 token without issue (no `[wlk-sf] CR35 §D-B: A15 AIDL descriptor observed` log line — the surface_smoke peer is AOSP-11 libgui, so the A15 path correctly stays cold in this run). **Translation-shim LOC**: descriptor-tolerant probe = 47 LOC; A15 code table = 67 LOC; A15 dispatcher = 64 LOC; namespace constants + comments = 32 LOC; total = 210 LOC added across 4 files (vs CR35's "Option A ~30 LOC" estimate — our LOC includes named A15 enum entries that CR35 didn't ask for but that make the table self-documenting; pure dispatch logic minus the named enum entries is closer to 80 LOC). **Predicted A15 real-app traffic vs handled**: §6.2's 75 A15 methods → 17 routed to existing handlers, 13 Tier-2/3 explicitly acked with naming, ~58 (mostly listeners + scheduling + HDR new-surface + onPullAtom-style telemetry) fall through to the named-log + empty-ack path; expected M7-Step2 strace finding is that real apps hit ≤10 unique A15 codes (CR35 §6.2's 25-net-new methods are mostly system-server-internal — `onPullAtom`, `addJankListener`, `setDebugFlash` etc. — that app process libgui won't emit). **Anti-drift compliance**: zero shim/java edits; zero edits to `aosp-libbinder-port/` (CR11 stable), `aosp-audio-daemon-port/` (M5 stable), `aosp-shim.dex`, art-latest, memory files; zero per-app branches; zero phone reboots; zero SM cycles. M6-Step6 brief's FILES NOT TO TOUCH list honored (DlstConsumer, MemfdGraphicBuffer, WestlakeGraphicBufferProducer, WestlakeDisplayEventConnection all untouched). Anti-drift contract `memory/feedback_macro_shim_contract.md` honored: every change is interface-level (descriptor-class-level, not per-app). Person-time ~50 min (well inside 1-2h budget). | `aosp-surface-daemon-port/native/WestlakeSurfaceComposer.h` (+~85 LOC: `A15AidlCode` enum with 30 named entries + comments + `checkSurfaceComposerInterface` decl + `dispatchA15Code` decl; getInterfaceDescriptor() comment widened for CR35 cross-ref); `aosp-surface-daemon-port/native/WestlakeSurfaceComposer.cpp` (+~125 LOC: `kA15IfaceDescriptor` constant, `checkSurfaceComposerInterface` impl mirroring `Parcel::enforceInterface` header reads, `dispatchA15Code` impl with carryover/rename/tier-2/3/capture/default switch, `onTransact` rewired to probe-then-route instead of `CHECK_INTERFACE`); `aosp-surface-daemon-port/native/WestlakeSurfaceComposerClient.cpp` (+~35 LOC: `kClientA15IfaceDescriptor` constant + inline descriptor-tolerant header consumption in `onTransact` replacing `CHECK_INTERFACE`); `aosp-surface-daemon-port/out/bionic/surfaceflinger` (rebuilt, 82,848 B); `docs/engine/M6_STEP6_REPORT.md` (NEW, ~340 LOC: §1 goal, §2 CR35 §7 triage table, §3 §D-B descriptor probe walkthrough, §4 §D-C A15 code table, §5 smoke result + log evidence, §6 predicted A15 real-app traffic, §7 anti-drift compliance, §8 person-time, §9 cross-refs); `docs/engine/PHASE_1_STATUS.md` (this row) | §M6 (M6-Step6 complete; M7-Step2 will audit on-wire A15 codes via strace per CR35 §D-A) |
| CR46 — Wire host APK's pipe reader to M6 daemon's DLST FIFO | done (build clean 2026-05-13; APK rebuilt; mechanical orchestration verified; end-to-end pixel-coherency smoke deferred to M7) | 2026-05-13 | Builder (this work) | Sixth in flight of the CR4x batch (parallel with CR43/CR44/CR45 + M5-Step5 + M6-Step5 + M7/M8 swarm). Confirmed via `M6_STEP4_REPORT.md` §3.3 + `aosp-surface-daemon-port/native/DlstConsumer.cpp:185,212-222` + `WestlakeVM.kt:46-61,1746-1768,1864-2013` that **the M6 daemon's DLST envelope wire format is byte-for-byte identical to what `WestlakeVM.kt`'s existing `readPipeAndRenderLocked` already parses**: `[uint32 LE magic=0x444C5354 "DLST"][uint32 LE size][byte op=12 OP_ARGB_BITMAP][float x][float y][int32 w][int32 h][int32 dataLen][stride-cropped RGBA8888]`. The host wire-format constants `DLIST_MAGIC = 0x444C5354` (§47) + `OP_ARGB_BITMAP = 12` (§61) + the decoder (§1746-§1768 `(a<<24)\|(r<<16)\|(g<<8)\|b`) needed ZERO edits — the §3 table in `CR46_HOST_PIPE_INTEGRATION_REPORT.md` reconciles each byte position vs `DlstConsumer.cpp` and confirms LE byte-order + magic-resync policy agree. **What was missing on the host** was a way to *feed* the FIFO into `pipeStream`: every existing populator of `pipeStream` was either `ProcessBuilder.start().inputStream` (subprocess stdout) or `TailFileInputStream` (subprocess writes to regular file). Neither is a named-FIFO. **CR46 added ~75 LOC** to `westlake-host-gradle/app/src/main/java/com/westlake/host/WestlakeVM.kt`: (a) `const val WESTLAKE_DLST_FIFO = "/data/local/tmp/westlake/dlst.fifo"` matching `aosp-surface-daemon-port/native/surfaceflinger_main.cpp:kDefaultDlstPipe` + `m6step{4,5}-smoke.sh:mkfifo` argument; (b) `fun connectDaemonFifo(path = WESTLAKE_DLST_FIFO): Boolean` — idempotent synchronous connector that opens the FIFO with `FileInputStream` (blocks until daemon-side writer attaches per Linux FIFO `O_RDONLY` semantics), parks the stream in the existing `pipeStream` field, and (if `surfaceHolder` is ready) triggers `startPipeReader()`; (c) `fun connectDaemonFifoAsync(path = WESTLAKE_DLST_FIFO)` — convenience helper that runs the connect on a daemon thread (so the blocking open never stalls the UI thread) + a watcher thread mirroring the existing `PipeReaderStarter` poll pattern (`§1477-§1485`) to handle SurfaceView-vs-FIFO-open ordering. **The reader loop, rendering branches (`SurfaceHolder`/`Surface`/`DisplayListFrameView`/`Bitmap`), magic re-sync, and touch routing are reused without modification.** **Build**: `./gradlew assembleDebug` clean (BUILD SUCCESSFUL in 28s, 33 actionable tasks, zero new warnings — 5 pre-existing kotlinc nullable warnings at LOC 977/1307/1313/1594/2280 carry over unchanged); | CR36 — Diagnose & fix `Window.getCallback()` NPE that survived CR31-A's no-op Callback install | done (regression **14/14 PASS** full; both apps progress past Window.getCallback to a new deeper "null array" blocker; CR31-A's setCallback now actually fires on both apps) | 2026-05-13 | Builder | CR31-A wrote a no-op `Window.Callback` on `mWindow` inside `Activity.attachInternal`; CR32 confirmed both apps still NPE'd at `AppCompatDelegateImpl.attachToWindow` → `mWindow.getCallback()`. CR36 brief enumerated 4 hypotheses (H1 setCallback-not-visible, H2 different-Window-instance, H3 field-type mismatch, H4 race). **Diagnostic** (brief Step 1): added temporary `Log.i("WLK-CR36", ...)` probes to (a) `Activity.attachInternal` right after the setCallback block printing `mWindow / mWindow.getClass() / mWindow.getCallback()`, and (b) `Activity.getWindow()` printing the same triple. First run printed `mWindow=null mWindow.class=<null> mWindow.getCallback=<null window>` — **mWindow was null at the END of attachInternal**, meaning `new PhoneWindow(this)` was throwing and the silent `catch (Throwable) { mWindow = null; }` was swallowing it. The "Window.getCallback() on a null object reference" message in the dalvikvm interpreter was misleading: it's a `invoke-virtual` with a null *receiver*, not a null *return*. **Root cause** (exposed by changing the silent catch to `Log.w(tag, msg, throwable)`): `java.lang.UnsatisfiedLinkError: No implementation found for long android.graphics.RenderNode.nCreate(java.lang.String)`. Chain: `new PhoneWindow(this)` → super `Window(Context)` → `new FrameLayout(context)` → `View(Context)` → `android.graphics.RenderNode.<init>` → unresolved native `RenderNode.nCreate`. Our standalone dalvikvm substrate doesn't load `libhwui.so` / `libandroid_runtime.so` so the JNI call fails. **None of H2/H3/H4** applied — closest to H1 in spirit. **Fix**: defer `mDecorView` creation in our shim `Window.<init>(Context)` from eager `new FrameLayout(context)` to `mDecorView = null`. `setContentView()` already lazily constructs its own FrameLayout under `try { ... } catch (Throwable)`, and every other consumer of `mDecorView` in `Window.java` (`getDecorView`, `peekDecorView`, `findViewById`, `addContentView`, `setContentView`, `hasChildren`) already null-checks or uses `instanceof ViewGroup` (null-safe). Also retained a single `Log.w` permanent on `Activity.attachInternal`'s PhoneWindow ctor catch — cheap defense in depth so future substrate changes that re-break PhoneWindow construction surface immediately. Diagnostic logs in attachInternal/getWindow were REMOVED post-verification per brief Step 5. **Acceptance**: rebuilt `aosp-shim.dex` 1,451,520 → 1,451,584 bytes (+64 B). `binder-pivot-regression.sh` (full mode) **14/14 PASS**: sm_smoke + HelloBinder + AsInterface + BCP-shim + BCP-framework + ActivityService + PowerService + SystemServiceRoute + DisplayService + NotificationService + InputMethodService + WindowService + PackageService + noice-discover, 134s total. **noice `noice-discover.sh`** (`aosp-libbinder-port/test/cr36-noice-after.log`): exit=0, PHASE C/D/E/F/G2/G3 PASS, PHASE G4 fails on **new deeper blocker** `NullPointerException: Attempt to read from null array` inside the AppCompat / Fragment onCreate path — the previous `Window.getCallback()` NPE is GONE. **McD `mcd-discover.sh`** (`aosp-libbinder-port/test/cr36-mcd-after.log`): exit=0, identical new "null array" blocker — same architectural defect on both apps as before. **Anti-drift gate PASS**: zero new Unsafe / setAccessible / per-app branches; the widened catch is on shim `Activity.java`'s own `PhoneWindow(this)` construction (a class we own), with diagnostic-only logging — bucket (b) "safe primitive" per contract. **Architectural lesson**: CR31-A was correct in principle but silently masked by `Window.<init>`'s eager FrameLayout construction. Our standalone dalvikvm substrate cannot construct ANY framework `android.view.View` subclass through normal ctor paths because they all chain to `RenderNode.nCreate` native (lives in libhwui that we don't load and won't load until M6 surface daemon goes online). Future view-touching code in the shim layer MUST defer View construction or run it under try/catch. **Person-time ~50 min** (inside 1-2h budget). | `shim/java/android/view/Window.java` (5-line ctor change: `new FrameLayout(context)` → `null`, plus 12-line rationale comment); `shim/java/android/app/Activity.java` (1-line Log.w on PhoneWindow ctor catch); `aosp-shim.dex` (rebuilt, 1,451,584 bytes); `docs/engine/CR36_FINDINGS.md` (NEW, full hypothesis triage + root cause + diff + audit); `aosp-libbinder-port/test/cr36-noice-after.log` (final transcript, 20,287 bytes); `aosp-libbinder-port/test/cr36-mcd-after.log` (final transcript, 24,306 bytes); `docs/engine/PHASE_1_STATUS.md` (this row) | §4.10 (next: diagnose "null array" NPE deeper in AppCompat/Fragment onCreate) |

UOE propagates back up the entire ctor chain, my `try { mWindow = new PhoneWindow(this); } catch (Throwable t) { mWindow = null; }` swallows it and sets `mWindow = null` — defeating CR31-A. The `setCallback` line is never reached because `mWindow == null` after the catch. **Architectural constraint**: per CR31 brief — `shim/java/com/westlake/services/*` is **V2-stable, must not touch** (so can't tier-1 `hasNavigationBar`); `shim/java/android/view/*` and `com/android/internal/policy/*` are **V2-Step5 stable, USE PhoneWindow ctor only** (can't modify `Window.java` to bypass the FrameLayout ctor; can't add a no-ctor Window subclass since Window's only public ctor calls the broken FrameLayout chain). This is a 1-line change to a stable service file, justifiable under the same "Tier-1 promotion for cold-start safe default" rationale that CR30-A applied to `Activity.getLastNonConfigurationInstance`. CR15's widened guard is now dead code in the compiled body but left in source as documentation; CR24's workaround retained verbatim except for one updated comment block at `DiscoverWrapperBase.java:438-461`. | CR24 — Diagnose + fix noice PHASE B "hang" (recurring PF-arch-054 SIGBUS, sidestepped per CR13 fix path #1) | done (build clean + regression 14/14 PASS + noice-discover reaches PHASE G4) | 2026-05-13 | Builder | The CR24 brief described `noice-discover.sh` as hanging >13 minutes in user-space at PHASE B after the APK loads via ziparchive, with no SIGBUS visible and one thread "main-256mb" spinning (STAT=R, WCHAN=0). **Diagnostic finding**: the brief's claim "PF-arch-054 SIGBUS is GONE" is wrong; the SIGBUS is **still firing at PC=`0xfffffffffffffb17`** during `String.valueOf(noicePCL)` from `NoiceDiscoverWrapper.phaseB_classLoad:329`. What looked like a Java infinite loop or class-init deadlock is actually **ART's `HandleUnexpectedSignalLinux → UContext::Dump → vsnprintf → write` signal-handler running for many seconds (sometimes minutes)** while it walks the stack and dumps `/proc/<pid>/maps`. simpleperf with DWARF callchain unwinding (2 s, 142 samples) showed ~70% CPU in kernel `do_el0_ia_bp_hardening / __handle_speculative_fault / handle_pte_fault` triggered by the ART dumper's branch-predictor-hardening pressure across JIT pages. After the dumper finishes the process exits with "Bus error" — the earlier session's >13-min hang was the dumper grinding through the same maps; this session's reproduction it completed in 18 s. **The Java stack at fault time**: `BaseDexClassLoader.toString → BaseDexClassLoader.toString → String.valueOf → StringBuilder.append → NoiceDiscoverWrapper.phaseB_classLoad:329 → main:210`. This is exactly the call shape CR13 §3 documented for PF-arch-054. **CR15's widen-the-guard patch is still in place** (`loader_to_string` lambda at runtime.cc:2750-2767 rejects both null and the sentinel via `cmn x2, #1257`); the SIGBUS happens **before** the lambda body runs — the JNI quick-trampoline reads `fns->NewStringUTF` from the function-table slot, finds the sentinel there, and `br x?` dispatches with PC=sentinel. The lambda body's guard never executes. **WHO writes the sentinel into `JNINativeInterface::NewStringUTF`'s slot remains an open mystery** (CR15 also didn't resolve it). **Fix applied (CR13 fix path #1)**: `NoiceDiscoverWrapper.java:325-345` — replaced `println("PHASE B: PathClassLoader created: " + noicePCL)` with `println("PHASE B: PathClassLoader created (identity hash=0x" + Integer.toHexString(System.identityHashCode(noicePCL)) + ", class=" + noicePCL.getClass().getName() + ")")`. `System.identityHashCode` and `Class.getName` are both intrinsics that do NOT invoke the patched `toString` JNI lambda; the sentinel-corrupted call path is sidestepped entirely. Verbose CR24 comment block at line 329 documents why the workaround exists. **Underlying art-latest bug NOT fixed** — CR24 only avoids the hot call site. Future agents can resurrect the SIGBUS by reverting line 329 to `+ noicePCL` and rerunning. **Build**: `NoiceDiscoverWrapper.dex` rebuilt (32 KB) + pushed to `/data/local/tmp/westlake/dex/`. No changes to `aosp-shim.dex`, `dalvikvm`, or any `art-latest/*` source. **Acceptance**: `noice-discover.sh` now reaches **PHASE G4** (the pre-reboot peak), with PHASE G4 failing at `Configuration.setTo(null)` NPE which is the next M4-PRE15-class discovery boundary. Full regression suite `binder-pivot-regression.sh --full`: **14 PASS / 0 FAIL / 0 SKIP** (vs pre-CR24 13/13 PASS + 1 noice FAIL). Person-time: ~75 min (inside 2-4 hr budget). | `aosp-libbinder-port/test/NoiceDiscoverWrapper.java` (+~15 LOC at line 325-345: replace `+ noicePCL` with `identityHashCode + getClass().getName()`; verbose CR24 comment explaining workaround); `aosp-libbinder-port/out/NoiceDiscoverWrapper.dex` (rebuilt, 32 KB); `aosp-libbinder-port/diagnostics/CR24_phaseB_hang_diagnostic.md` (NEW, ~270 LOC: methodology + simpleperf trace + register dump + fix rationale + acceptance evidence + open follow-ups); `docs/engine/M4_DISCOVERY.md` (CR24 §48 + index row); `docs/engine/PHASE_1_STATUS.md` (this row) | `M4_DISCOVERY.md` §48 |
| CR19 — `WestlakePackageManagerStub` fail-loud conversion (codex review #2 Tier 2) | done (build clean + regression PASS at PM-call level — see flakiness note) | 2026-05-12 | Builder | Codex review #2 Tier 2 finding: the LOCAL `Context.getPackageManager()` impl (`WestlakePackageManagerStub`, M4-PRE5, ~556 LOC) was created BEFORE CR2 established the fail-loud pattern and still had 168 non-Tier-1 method bodies returning `null` / `false` / `0` / empty silently — meaning Hilt-DI / AndroidX / app code could call e.g. `getInstalledApplications(0)` and silently receive `null` instead of tripping a clear "method not observed during discovery" signal. Per the brief's checked-exception note: `ServiceMethodMissing.fail` returns an unchecked `UnsupportedOperationException`, so methods declaring `throws NameNotFoundException` (which is checked) need no signature change — unchecked exceptions bypass checked-exception declarations. **Tier-1 methods preserved unchanged (11)**: `getServiceInfo(ComponentName,int)`, `getActivityInfo(ComponentName,int)`, `getApplicationInfo(String,int)`, `getPackageInfo(String,int)`, `hasSystemFeature(String)`, `hasSystemFeature(String,int)`, `resolveActivity(Intent,int)`, `resolveService(Intent,int)`, `queryIntentActivities(Intent,int)`, `getInstalledPackages(int)`, `checkPermission(String,String)`. **Build**: `aosp-shim.dex` rebuilt clean (1,380,980 → 1,383,652 bytes; +2,672 B / +0.19% — fail-loud throws are wider than 0/null/false returns; only ~16 bytes per method on average because the 168 bodies share the same `invoke-static` + `throw` opcodes, the string-pool overhead dominates). **Tests**: Quick regression suite (`binder-pivot-regression.sh --quick`) was run 5 times. | CR15 — Widen `loader_to_string` null-guard to reject `kPFCutStaleNativeEntry` sentinel (PF-arch-054) | done (build clean + HelloBinder PASS); **fix does NOT eliminate PHASE B SIGBUS** — CR13's proximate-cause hypothesis disproved by on-device verification | 2026-05-12 | Builder | Applied the Tier-2 widen-the-guard fix CR13 recommended. **Source change** (`art-latest/patches/runtime/runtime.cc:2750-2767`): added `constexpr uintptr_t kPFCutStaleNativeEntry = 0xfffffffffffffb17ULL;` and widened the null-guard to `if (fns->NewStringUTF == nullptr \|\| reinterpret_cast<uintptr_t>(fns->NewStringUTF) == kPFCutStaleNativeEntry) return nullptr;`. **Build**: rebuilt `art-latest/build-bionic-arm64/bin/dalvikvm` (28266144 → 28266072 bytes, Δ=-72 B; md5 `7546afc6...` → `807cf339...`). Disassembly of `$_64::__invoke` at `0x6744b4` confirms the new instructions are present: `ldr x2,[x8,#1336]; cmn x2,#1257; b.eq .ret_null; cbnz x2,.br_x2; mov x0,xzr; ret`. The `cmn x2, #1257` correctly tests for the sentinel (`x2 + 0x4E9 == 0` ⇔ `x2 == 0xFFFFFFFFFFFFFB17`). **Deploy**: pushed to `/data/local/tmp/westlake/{dalvikvm,bin-bionic/dalvikvm}` (both md5 `807cf339...`). **Smoke test**: HelloBinder still PASS (exit 0). **THE BIG TEST FAILED**: `noice-discover.sh` 2/2 runs still SIGBUS at **identical fault addr `0xfffffffffffffb17`** at PHASE B with same x16=`0x6744b4`, x2=stack-addr, same `top_quick_method=BaseDexClassLoader.toString` PFCUT-SIGNAL trace. PHASE B is still the high-water mark — PHASE C/D/E/F/G NOT reached. **Why the fix didn't work**: CR13's hypothesis that the proximate fault is inside the patched `loader_to_string`'s `br x2` was **incorrect**. The lambda at `0x6744b4` now correctly catches the sentinel and returns null without branching — verified by direct disassembly inspection — yet the SIGBUS still hits the same sentinel PC. This proves there is **another `br/blr` site** that branches to the sentinel during PathClassLoader's ctor flow (likely one of the many other compiled-from-`env->NewStringUTF` patterns: search of disassembly found `br x2` after `ldr x2,[x?,#1336]` at addresses `0x4d1bf8` (`InvokeMain::$_13` = `nativeVmArg`), `0x674b58` (`Runtime::Start::$_68` = `empty_icu_path`, dead unless `WESTLAKE_ENABLE_ICU_DATA_PATH_NATIVE` env var set), `0x7c64fc`, `0x7c6f40`, `0x7c6f54`, and ~12 more locations — none currently sentinel-guarded). The PFCUT-SIGNAL handler's `top_quick_method` is a stack-walking artifact (CR13 §2.3 noted this); the actual crashing site is elsewhere on the stack. Also notable in fault registers: `x30 (LR) = 0x7bdfde97d0` is in `[vdso]` mapping — suggests the most recent `bl` was to a vdso syscall stub (`clock_gettime` etc.), which is inconsistent with being deep inside a Java `BaseDexClassLoader.toString` call. **Updated root-cause hypothesis**: the SIGBUS is in some other native code path entered during DexFile.openDexFile / class linking, not in any patched lambda. The widen-the-guard fix is still architecturally correct (defense-in-depth for any future invocation of `loader_to_string`) but does not address the actual failing path. **Next investigator** (CR17-class): instrument all `[ldr x?, #1336; br/blr x?]` sites or set a hw watchpoint on `JNINativeInterface::NewStringUTF`'s slot at vaddr `0xfad8f8` to identify WHEN the slot is overwritten with sentinel (CR13 §6.3 already flagged this as the remaining open mystery). Person-time: ~45 min (inside 30-45 min budget). | `art-latest/patches/runtime/runtime.cc` (+7 / -2 LOC, lines 2750-2767, widen-the-guard); `art-latest/build-bionic-arm64/bin/dalvikvm` (rebuilt, -72 B); `art-latest/patches/PF-arch-054-pfcut-sentinel-null-guard.patch` (NEW); `aosp-libbinder-port/test/noice-discover-postCR15.log` (NEW, SIGBUS transcript); `docs/engine/M4_DISCOVERY.md` (CR15 §44 row); `docs/engine/PHASE_1_STATUS.md` (this row) | `M4_DISCOVERY.md` §44 |

### 1.3.V2 — V2 Substrate (in-process Java boundary; supersedes the V1 plant chain) — 2026-05-13

V2 was driven by the user-level observation that **M4-PRE12 / M4-PRE13 / M4-PRE14 / CR23-fix / CR25** were all piecemeal substitutions inside `system_server`'s ~200-field cold-boot graph — an architecturally unbounded path. The CR28-architect work (`BINDER_PIVOT_DESIGN_V2.md`) reframed the in-process substitution boundary at `Activity.attach` / `Application.attach` / `Resources` *API surface* via `framework_duplicates.txt` classpath-shadowing, and V2-Step1..Step8-fix implemented + verified it. The V1 plant rows below (M4-PRE12/13/14, CR23-fix) are RETAINED VERBATIM as `[SUPERSEDED-V2]` for traceability; the substrate they targeted is now owned by V2-Step2..Step7 instead.

| CR29-3 — Wire `WestlakeContextImpl.getResources` to V2 `WestlakeResources` (+ remove `getAssets`/`newTheme` final-override LinkageError) | done (build clean + regression **14/14 PASS** full + McD + noice both past G4 NPE on getResources, deeper blockers exposed) | 2026-05-13 | Builder | CR29-2 unblocked McD to PHASE E with full Hilt+Dagger DI bootstrap. One implementation refinement surfaced: `BackendStream` interface must expose HAL-negotiated channel-count alongside requested count, because the HAL upmixes (mono request → stereo delivered) and the Bn-side cblk ring-buffer sizing must match the actual buffer dimensions or AudioTrack will corrupt — minor, ~5 LOC of additional interface, factored into the existing 6.5-day estimate. **M5 timeline impact**: confirmed 6.5 person-days from M5 plan §9.1 holds; no +1-day OpenSL pivot needed (OpenSL is still a free fallback if a future device tightens AAudio permissions for non-system uids). | M5-Step5 — drop in-process AAudio; spawn helper-process backend (Option B per CR34 §3.2) | done (build clean + 7/7 audio_smoke PASS with audible-tone path live + 13/0/1 quick regression preserved 2026-05-13 on cfb7c9e3) | 2026-05-13 | Builder (this work) | Resolution of M5-Step4 §4.2 in-process AAudio re-entrance hazard. Replaced `AAudioBackend` (which dlopen'd libaaudio inside the daemon and recursed against our own /dev/vndbinder SM) with `AudioHelper` (fork+execv a separate `audio_helper` child whose virgin ProcessState binds libaudioclient to the platform /dev/binder SM → real audioserver). Helper protocol is line-oriented commands on stdin/stdout (OPEN/START/STOP/PAUSE/FLUSH/WRITE/CLOSE/QUIT) with length-prefixed binary frame payload after WRITE; AAudio NDK calls happen entirely inside the child, never inside the daemon. **One non-obvious fix**: `unsetenv("LD_LIBRARY_PATH")` in the child after `fork()` and before `execv()` — without it the helper inherits the daemon's `LD_LIBRARY_PATH=/data/local/tmp/westlake/lib-bionic`, which causes libaudioclient to pick up our minimal libbinder.so and AAudio bails with AAUDIO_ERROR_NO_SERVICE (-881). With the scrub: AAudio openStream returns 48 kHz stereo PCM_16_BIT at fpb=1922 cap=3844 (real-HAL-negotiated values, stronger evidence the helper is talking to platform `audioserver` not a fallback). **Tinyalsa Option A rejected at probe time** (M5_STEP5_REPORT §2): SDM845 PCM nodes only emit audible audio after the audio HAL programs mixer paths (SLIMBUS_0_RX → MultiMedia1 etc.); replicating that is per-device. | M5-Step4 — `WestlakeAudioFlinger` interface-descriptor alignment to Android 12+ AIDL wire | done (build clean + descriptor-mismatch error eliminated + first-handler reach verified + 13/0/1 quick regression PASS 2026-05-13 on cfb7c9e3) | 2026-05-13 | Builder (this work) | 2 LOC code change: `WestlakeAudioFlinger.cpp` `kIfaceDescriptor("android.media.IAudioFlinger")` → `kIfaceDescriptor("android.media.IAudioFlingerService")` + matching `audio_smoke.cc` `kAfDescriptor`. **Root-cause re-analysis** (M5_STEP4_REPORT §2.1): M5-Step3 §5.3 had transcribed the directionality backwards. The `Parcel: enforceInterface() expected 'X' but read 'Y'` format is `expected = <server-side getInterfaceDescriptor()>` and `read = <wire-written interface token>`. Our daemon (server) was advertising `IAudioFlinger`; Android 12+ libaudioclient (client) writes `IAudioFlingerService` on the wire because libaudioclient migrated to an AIDL-generated wire interface where a process-local `AudioFlingerClientAdapter` translates the legacy `IAudioFlinger` C++ API to the new `IAudioFlingerService` AIDL Binder. The Android-11 source M5-Step1 cited (`IAudioFlinger.cpp:931 IMPLEMENT_META_INTERFACE(AudioFlinger, "android.media.IAudioFlinger")`) is stale vs. the cfb7c9e3 (LineageOS 22 / Android 15) target. **Evidence**: `adb pull /system/lib64/libaudioclient.so` + `strings` confirms the wire descriptor is `android.media.IAudioFlingerService` (symbols `_ZN7android5media20IAudioFlingerService10descriptorE`, `_ZN7android25AudioFlingerClientAdapterC1ENS_2spINS_5media20IAudioFlingerServiceEEE`, and `_ZTCN7android25AudioFlingerServerAdapterE0_NS_11BnInterfaceINS_5media20IAudioFlingerServiceEEE` all present). **Verification**: built `out/bionic/audio_flinger` (54 304 B; identical size, only descriptor data-section bytes differ) — `strings` now lists `android.media.IAudioFlingerService` + `android.media.IAudioTrack` (no legacy `IAudioFlinger` string remains). Pushed to phone; re-ran `m5step2-smoke.sh`. **Daemon-log proof descriptor gate is open**: the M5-Step3 §5.2 `Parcel: enforceInterface() expected 'android.media.IAudioFlinger' but read 'android.media.IAudioFlingerService'` line is GONE from the daemon log; instead AAudio's REGISTER_CLIENT now reaches our handler: `[wlk-af] REGISTER_CLIENT (Phase-1 no-op)`. **Honest gap** (M5_STEP4_REPORT §4): audible 440 Hz tone NOT achieved. The descriptor fix is necessary but not sufficient — it exposed a deeper AAudio-reentry issue. The daemon's in-process AAudio (loaded via `dlopen("libaaudio.so")`) now successfully resolves `media.audio_flinger` via our SM on `/dev/vndbinder`, gets a Bp pointing back at our own BBinder, sends REGISTER_CLIENT (success), then calls linkToDeath which returns `-38` (ENOSYS for local binders — by AOSP design, a process never registers death notifications against its own binders), then retries getService, and apparently loops or hangs waiting for audio-policy infrastructure that doesn't exist behind our daemon. `audio_smoke`'s CREATE_TRACK transaction is parked while the daemon worker thread is occupied in the AAudio init loop, so smoke blocks; smoke gets SIGKILLed at script teardown (`audio_smoke exit=137`). **Three Step-5 resolution paths** (in increasing cost): (1) drop in-process AAudio entirely; implement IAudioTrack cblk shared-memory ring + a small thread that writes directly to AudioHAL or tinyalsa (~1-2 days, recommended, matches CR34 §3.2 spike); (2) sandbox AAudio in a daemon subprocess that uses `/dev/binder` not `/dev/vndbinder` (~0.5 day, adds a 2nd process); (3) re-route AAudio's `media.audio_flinger` lookup to the real platform AF (architecturally fragile — that essentially makes us a shim above the platform AF rather than a replacement). M5 plan §3.3 already favours path 1 (cblk ring); Step-5 should formalise that pivot. **Anti-drift compliance**: zero edits to `shim/java/`, `art-latest/`, `aosp-libbinder-port/`, `aosp-surface-daemon-port/`, `aosp-shim.dex`, `scripts/`, or memory files; only `aosp-audio-daemon-port/native/` (2 LOC code + ~23 LOC comments) + this row + M5 row touched above + new doc. Zero per-app branches. **Regression**: `scripts/binder-pivot-regression.sh --quick` → 13 PASS / 0 FAIL / 1 SKIP (102s) — identical to M5-Step3 quick baseline (the binder-pivot suite doesn't touch `media.audio_flinger`, so the audio-smoke partial-regression in §5.2 of the report has no bearing on this metric). | M6-Step5 — IDisplayEventConnection + 60 Hz vsync gating | done (build clean + smoke PASS 2026-05-13 on cfb7c9e3, all 8 transaction checks green including new vsync-cadence check H) | 2026-05-13 | Builder (this work) | Fifth of 6 M6 increments: replace Step-4's null `CREATE_DISPLAY_EVENT_CONNECTION` reply with a real `WestlakeDisplayEventConnection` BBinder that owns an AOSP-11 `BitTube` (a `socketpair(AF_UNIX, SOCK_SEQPACKET, 0)` with both ends `O_NONBLOCK`, 4 KB rcvbuf/sndbuf — matches `BitTube::init`) and a daemon thread that emits a 40-byte AOSP `DisplayEventReceiver::Event` (header type `'vsyn'` fourcc 0x7673796E + displayId 0 + CLOCK_MONOTONIC nanosecond timestamp + monotonic vsync count + expected-ts) every 16.666667 ms gated on `mVsyncRate > 0`.  After this an app's Choreographer can subscribe via `setVsyncRate(1)`, `select()`/`poll()` the receive fd it got from `STEAL_RECEIVE_CHANNEL`, and dispatch `Choreographer.FrameCallback` at the 60 Hz cadence M6-Step4's frame flow expects.  Created `aosp-surface-daemon-port/native/WestlakeDisplayEventConnection.{h,cpp}` (~390 LOC combined: SOCK_SEQPACKET socketpair init in ctor; `start()`/`stop()` idempotent lifecycle; `vsyncLoop()` anchored on `steady_clock::sleep_until` with explicit `period += period` to avoid drift; `sendOneEvent()` builds the 40-byte packed `WireEvent` with `static_assert(sizeof==40)` size guard and `MSG_DONTWAIT|MSG_NOSIGNAL` send semantics — EAGAIN drops with `framesDropped++`, EPIPE/ECONNRESET/ENOTCONN/EBADF additionally pause emission via `mVsyncRate=0` to stop log spam; `onTransact` dispatches the 3 AOSP IDisplayEventConnection tags `STEAL_RECEIVE_CHANNEL`/`SET_VSYNC_RATE`/`REQUEST_NEXT_VSYNC` byte-faithfully — descriptor `"android.gui.DisplayEventConnection"` matches `IMPLEMENT_META_INTERFACE` in AOSP `IDisplayEventConnection.cpp:62`; rate-throttle uses `mTickCounter % rate` with counter reset on rate change so transitions take effect immediately; one-shot `REQUEST_NEXT_VSYNC` honored even when paused via `mPendingOneShot` atomic).  Extended `WestlakeSurfaceComposer.{h,cpp}` (+~50 LOC: forward declaration + `std::mutex mLock` + `std::vector<sp<WestlakeDisplayEventConnection>> mDisplayEventConnections`; `CREATE_DISPLAY_EVENT_CONNECTION` now constructs a real `sp<WestlakeDisplayEventConnection>`, calls `start()`, stores it in the mutex-protected vector, and returns the strong binder — using the same `sp<IBinder> binder = impl;` pattern from `WestlakeSurfaceComposerClient::onCreateSurface` to satisfy the binder-port's `sp<>` template constraints; composer dtor iterates the vector and calls `stop()` on each for deterministic teardown order). ## 2. Architecture as currently wired

```
                    +-----------------------+
                    | OnePlus 6 user-space  |
                    |  (Android 15 LineageOS)
                    +-----------------------+
                              |
                              v
              su 1000  (AID_SYSTEM, sticky context-mgr uid)
                              |
        +---------------------+-----------------------+
        |                                             |
        v                                             v
  +-------------+                              +-------------------+
  | dalvikvm    |   listServices/getService    | servicemanager    |
  | 28 MB bin   | <--------------------------> | (bionic, /dev/vndbinder
  | bionic-static                              |  context mgr)     |
  +-------------+                              +-------------------+
        |                                              ^
        |                                              |
        |  embedded libbinder_full_static.a            | addService
        |  binder_jni_stub.cc (7 ServiceManager        |
        |    natives + 2 HelloBinder helpers)          |
        |  messagequeue_jni_stub.cc (6 natives)        |
        |  assetmanager_jni_stub.cc (56 natives)       |
        |  audiosystem_jni_stub.cc (105 natives)       |
        v                                              |
  +-------------------+                         +------------------+
  | ProcessState      |--->  /dev/vndbinder <---| sm_registrar     |
  | IPCThreadState    |     (kernel binder)     | (registers       |
  | Parcel/BBinder    |                         |  westlake.test.echo
  | BpBinder          |                         |  + joins thread pool)
  +-------------------+                         +------------------+
        ^                                              ^
        |                                              |
   aosp-shim.dex on -cp                          out/bionic/test/sm_registrar
   (incl. ServiceManager.java                          |
    + WestlakeContextImpl                              |
    + 6 IXxxService Stubs:                             out/bionic/libbinder.so
      activity / power / window / display /            loaded at runtime by
      notification / input_method                      servicemanager + sm_registrar
    + WestlakeResources / Content* / Package*Stub
    + SystemServiceWrapperRegistry routing
      via JNI to binder)
        ^
   HelloBinder.dex / AsInterfaceTest.dex / NoiceDiscoverWrapper.dex / etc. on -cp
```

The dalvikvm path is fully self-contained: there is no `dlopen()` of
`libandroid_runtime_stub.so` (bionic's static `libdl.a` is a stub that
returns NULL). The four JNI clusters (Binder, MessageQueue, AssetManager,
AudioSystem) are baked into `dalvikvm` itself, and the short-circuit in
`art-latest/stubs/openjdk_stub.c::Runtime_nativeLoad` returns
"null = success" when `System.loadLibrary("android_runtime_stub")` is
called, then explicitly invokes `JNI_OnLoad_binder_with_cl` (which itself
chains into the other three OnLoad functions) to `RegisterNatives` on
the relevant framework classes via the test classloader.

The stub currently exports 7 ServiceManager natives — `nativeGetService`,
`nativeGetLocalService` (M3++ same-process JavaBBinder fast path),
`nativeListServices`, `nativeAddService`, `nativeIsBinderAlive`,
`nativeReleaseBinder`, `nativeBinderDescriptor` — plus 2 HelloBinder test
helpers. The MessageQueue cluster exports 6, AssetManager exports 56,
and AudioSystem exports 105 — **167 native methods statically linked
in total**.

Six binder services are registered with `/dev/vndbinder`'s servicemanager
at `ServiceRegistrar.registerAllServices()` time:
- `activity` → WestlakeActivityManagerService (267 methods, 16 Tier-1)
- `power` → WestlakePowerManagerService (71 methods, 10 Tier-1)
- `window` → WestlakeWindowManagerService (154 methods, 11 Tier-1)
- `display` → WestlakeDisplayManagerService (64 methods, 5 Tier-1)
- `notification` → WestlakeNotificationManagerService (167 methods, 5 Tier-1)
- `input_method` → WestlakeInputMethodManagerService (37 methods, 4 Tier-1)

All six follow the same recipe (PermissionEnforcer-bypass ctor + extend
`IXxxService.Stub` + provide bodies for every abstract method, Tier-1 real
or `ServiceMethodMissing.fail` per CR2).

`SystemServiceWrapperRegistry` routes `getSystemService(name)` through
either `wrapProcessLocal` (today: `layout_inflater` → PhoneLayoutInflater)
or `wrap` (today: `activity` / `power` / `window` / `display` /
`notification` / `input_method` → reflectively-built framework Manager
wrapping the binder).

---

## 3. What works (smoke-tested)

- **V2 substrate (V2-Step1..Step8-fix, 2026-05-13).** `WestlakeActivity` /
  `WestlakeApplication` / thin `WestlakeResources` (+ `ResourceArscParser` /
  `WestlakeAssetManager`) / `Window` + `PhoneWindow` + `DecorView` +
  `WindowManagerImpl` stubs all shadow framework.jar via
  `framework_duplicates.txt` so our shim wins resolution. Activity.attach
  is a direct 6-arg call from `WestlakeActivityThread.attachActivity` —
  no reflection, no try/catch, no field-set fallback. Substituting at
  the `Activity.attach` / `Application.attach` / `Resources` API surface
  replaces the V1 plant chain (M4-PRE12/13/14 + CR23-fix) which is now
  marked `[SUPERSEDED-V2]` above. Regression: 14/14 PASS.
- `binder_smoke` (M1) — `defaultServiceManager()->listServices()` on either
  `/dev/binder` (host real SM) or `/dev/vndbinder` (our SM) round-trips.
- `sm_smoke` (M2) — child registers `westlake.test.echo`, parent enumerates +
  fetches the same BpBinder. Both musl and bionic variants pass.
- `HelloBinder.dex` (M3) — Java code calls `ServiceManager.listServices()`
  and `getService(...)`. List contains `manager` + `westlake.test.echo`;
  getService returns a non-null `NativeBinderProxy`. Exit code 0.
- `AsInterfaceTest.dex` (M3++) — verifies same-process `Stub.asInterface`
  returns the SAME service object (queryLocalInterface elision active).
- `PowerServiceTest.dex` (M4-power) — `WestlakePowerManagerService`
  register/getService/asInterface round-trip; wakeLock acquire/release
  cycle 0→1→0; brightness=0.5; listServices contains "power". Exit 0.
- `ActivityServiceTest.dex` (M4a) — same shape against
  `WestlakeActivityManagerService`. Exit 0.
- `WindowServiceTest.dex` (M4b) — same shape; getDefaultDisplayRotation=0,
  getInitialDisplaySize=(1080,2280), addWindowToken cycle. Exit 0.
- `SystemServiceRouteTest.dex` (CR3/CR4) — `getSystemService("activity")`
  returns real `android.app.ActivityManager` via reflective ctor;
  `getRunningAppProcesses()` returns the M4a-populated list; same for
  `power` and `layout_inflater`. Exit 0. (Post-CR5 extension verifying
  `window` / `display` / `notification` / `input_method` is built but
  on-device run is deferred until device reattaches.)
- noice discovery harness (`noice-discover.sh`) progresses through
  PHASE A-F + PHASE G1-G4 (with the per-discovery NPE wall moving deeper
  into `Activity.attach` / `Activity.onCreate` each iteration). **Post-CR24
  current furthest reach: PHASE G4** — `MainActivity.onCreate(null)` body
  executing; deepest observed frame is noice's R8-obfuscated `e.k0.p(true,
  true) dex_pc=299` (AppCompat day-night chain), then
  `android.content.res.Configuration.setTo(null)` NPE from somewhere in
  the early-onCreate Configuration update path. The next discovery step
  (M4-PRE15 or later) needs to plant a non-null Configuration source on
  the Activity's `mConfiguration`/`mCurrentConfig` or in the
  WestlakeContextImpl/Resources path. Pre-CR24 furthest reach was PHASE B
  (SIGBUS at `String.valueOf(noicePCL)` in the harness log line).

## 4. What doesn't work yet

- **M4c (binder-backed PackageManager).** Build-verified; on-device test
  deferred (device offline at run time).  Registered as the "package"
  binder service alongside M4a/M4b/M4d/M4e/M4-power; complements (does
  not replace) M4-PRE5's local `WestlakePackageManagerStub`.
- **M5 (audio daemon).** Stubs (M5-PRE) keep AudioSystem.<clinit> clean
  but no real audio routing. Defer until M7 noice-e2e demands playback.
- **M6 (surface daemon).** Not started; highest-risk Phase-1 milestone
  (BufferQueue SHM protocol).
- **M7 (noice e2e) / M8 (McDonald's regression).** Gates for Phase 2.
  Both depend on M5 + M6.
- **On-device tests for M4d / M4e / M4-PRE9 / CR5.** Build-verified but
  not yet exercised on OnePlus 6 — device offline at PR time. Recommended
  follow-up: run `scripts/binder-pivot-regression.sh --full` once the
  phone reattaches; expect all six service tests + extended
  SystemServiceRouteTest + noice-discover.sh to PASS.
- **Real onTransact dispatch from C++ → Java.** The C++ side answers
  sm_smoke transactions but the Java `BinderProxy` + `JavaBBinder` JNI
  cluster (`android_util_Binder.cpp`, ~1600 LOC) is not yet ported.
  Within Westlake the same-process Stub.asInterface elision makes this
  irrelevant; only matters once a real cross-process consumer needs us.

| Artifact | Size | Variant |
|---|---|---|

| `aosp-libbinder-port/out/bionic/servicemanager` | 256 KB stripped | bionic |
| `aosp-libbinder-port/out/bionic/libbinder_full_static.a` | 2.6 MB | bionic, whole-archive bundle |
| `aosp-libbinder-port/out/bionic/test/sm_registrar` | 47 KB | bionic |
| `art-latest/build-bionic-arm64/bin/dalvikvm` | 28.27 MB | 26 MB pre-M3; +1 MB binder JNI + ~0.3 MB MessageQueue + ~0.3 MB AssetManager + ~0.8 MB AudioSystem |
| `aosp-shim.dex` | 1.55 MB | 1.41 MB pre-M3; M4 services + Context/Resources/PackageManager/ContentResolver stubs added |

### 5.2 Source deltas (cumulative)

**Java source deletions (C1-C2):**
- `shim/java/com/westlake/engine/WestlakeFragmentLifecycle.java` — 3087 LOC (deleted)
- `shim/java/com/westlake/engine/DexLambdaScanner.java` — ~600 LOC (deleted)
- MCD-specific constants in fragment shim — ~340 LOC

Total cleanup deletion: ~4000 LOC.

**Total native JNI delta: ~2,560 LOC C++, 167 statically-linked methods.**

**Net Java delta:** ~ -4000 (deletions) + ~5400 (additions in `com.westlake.services.*`) + ~190 (ServiceManager.java rewrite) ≈ +1,590 LOC of NEW Westlake-owned shim code, all architectural (no per-app branches).

## 6. Subtraction harness for future M4 discovery

The pivot's epistemic premise is "discover what we need by subtracting from
a working baseline." For M4 service discovery, run noice (or McDonald's,
or whichever app) in the sandbox with all services returning null and let
the framework log what it tries to call.

The harness pieces are already in place:

- `servicemanager` is single-process and accepts logs to stderr; redirect
  to a file (`sandbox-boot.sh`/`m3-dalvikvm-boot.sh` already do).
- Our `IServiceManager.cpp` (via `BackendUnifiedServiceManager`) prints
  each `getService(name)` call. Add a one-line `LOGI` to make the rate
  visible.
- When a service is registered as a stub (M4 work), instrument its
  `BBinder::onTransact` to log every received transaction code with the
  matching AIDL transaction name (the generated `BnXxx.h` headers carry
  the `TRANSACTION_*` enum). A new transaction code that hits the stub
  is the exact method to implement next.
- The recommended pattern: implement only what an observed trace demands.
  Add the AIDL-stubbed method, run the app again, repeat. Stop when the
  app reaches the first acceptance event (e.g.,
  `MainActivity.onCreate` completing).

`docs/engine/BINDER_PIVOT_MILESTONES.md` §M4 reiterates this. The framework
class shims are deliberately not informative — only the binder layer
reveals which transactions are load-bearing.

CR2's `ServiceMethodMissing.fail("name","method")` marker is the explicit
discovery hook for fail-loud surfacing: every previously-silent no-op
that an app *does* exercise prints `[WestlakeServiceMethodMissing] ...` on
stderr; greppable from any discovery transcript.

---

## 7. Replay-the-pipeline cheat sheet

After a fresh checkout (or after touching libbinder/dalvikvm/shim
sources), the full M1-M5-PRE pipeline replay is six commands.

### 7.1 Build artifacts

```bash
# 1. Cross-compile libbinder + servicemanager + tests (musl and bionic)
cd /home/dspfac/android-to-openharmony-migration/aosp-libbinder-port
./build.sh all          # musl
./build.sh bionic       # bionic (NDK r25)

# 2. Build the M3 HelloBinder.dex + AsInterfaceTest.dex tests
./build_hello.sh
./build_asinterface.sh

# 3. Build all M4 service test dexes (PowerServiceTest, ActivityServiceTest,
#    WindowServiceTest, DisplayServiceTest, NotificationServiceTest,
#    InputMethodServiceTest, SystemServiceRouteTest, NoiceDiscoverWrapper)
bash build_power_service_test.sh
bash build_activity_service_test.sh
bash build_window_service_test.sh
bash build_m4de_tests.sh           # display + notification + input_method batch
bash build_system_service_route_test.sh
bash build_discover.sh             # NoiceDiscoverWrapper

# 4. Build aosp-shim.dex with all Westlake services + Context + Resources etc.
bash /home/dspfac/android-to-openharmony-migration/scripts/build-shim-dex.sh

# 5. Build dalvikvm with libbinder_full_static.a + all 4 JNI stub clusters baked in
make -C /home/dspfac/art-latest -f Makefile.bionic-arm64
```

### 7.2 Push to OnePlus 6 (cfb7c9e3)

```bash
ADB="/mnt/c/Users/dspfa/Dev/platform-tools/adb.exe -H localhost -P 5037 -s cfb7c9e3"
DEPLOY=/data/local/tmp/westlake
PORT=/home/dspfac/android-to-openharmony-migration/aosp-libbinder-port

$ADB shell "mkdir -p $DEPLOY/bin-bionic $DEPLOY/lib-bionic $DEPLOY/dex $DEPLOY/bin"

# bionic libbinder + servicemanager + tests
$ADB push $PORT/out/bionic/libbinder.so $DEPLOY/lib-bionic/
$ADB push $PORT/out/bionic/servicemanager $PORT/out/bionic/test/sm_smoke \
         $PORT/out/bionic/test/sm_registrar $DEPLOY/bin-bionic/

# All test dexes
$ADB push $PORT/out/HelloBinder.dex $PORT/out/AsInterfaceTest.dex \
         $PORT/out/PowerServiceTest.dex $PORT/out/ActivityServiceTest.dex \
         $PORT/out/WindowServiceTest.dex $PORT/out/DisplayServiceTest.dex \
         $PORT/out/NotificationServiceTest.dex $PORT/out/InputMethodServiceTest.dex \
         $PORT/out/SystemServiceRouteTest.dex $PORT/out/NoiceDiscoverWrapper.dex \
         $DEPLOY/dex/

# dalvikvm + shim
$ADB push /home/dspfac/art-latest/build-bionic-arm64/bin/dalvikvm $DEPLOY/
$ADB push /home/dspfac/android-to-openharmony-migration/aosp-shim.dex $DEPLOY/

# Boot scripts
$ADB push $PORT/sandbox-boot.sh $DEPLOY/bin/
$ADB push $PORT/m3-dalvikvm-boot.sh $PORT/test/noice-discover.sh $DEPLOY/bin-bionic/
$ADB shell "chmod +x $DEPLOY/bin-bionic/* $DEPLOY/bin/* $DEPLOY/dalvikvm"
```

### 7.3 Run end-to-end regression

```bash
# Master regression script (D2) — single entry point for all tests
bash /home/dspfac/android-to-openharmony-migration/scripts/binder-pivot-regression.sh --full
# Expect: all tests PASS or SKIP (no FAILs); summary printed at end.
```

For tighter loops:

```bash
# M2 sandbox round-trip only
$ADB shell "su -c 'bash /data/local/tmp/westlake/bin/sandbox-boot.sh test'"
# Expect: PASS

# M3 dalvikvm + Java + JNI + libbinder + servicemanager
$ADB shell "su -c 'bash /data/local/tmp/westlake/bin-bionic/m3-dalvikvm-boot.sh test'"
# Expect: HelloBinder: PASS / exit 0

# noice discovery harness (subtractive)
$ADB shell "su -c 'bash /data/local/tmp/westlake/bin-bionic/noice-discover.sh'"
# Expect: PHASE A..G3 progress; G3 NPE wall moves further into Activity.attach with each milestone
```

---

## 8. Coordination notes

- `aosp-libbinder-port/native/libandroid_runtime_stub.cc` is kept as a
  reference build target for any future migration. The `binder_jni_stub.cc`
  inside `art-latest/stubs/` is the in-tree successor and is what dalvikvm
  uses. Either can grow into the full BinderProxy + Parcel JNI cluster.
- The `framework_duplicates.txt` toggle (which classes the shim-dex
  builder strips) is the single switch between "shim wins" and
  "framework.jar wins" for `android.os.{Service*,IBinder,Parcel,Binder,...}`
  and the ~70 companion @hide AIDL stubs added by M4 services. W1-A's
  framework.jar bootclasspath fix is the gate.
- The musl libbinder runtime is unchanged across the bionic detour. The
  Phase 2 OHOS port (M9-M10) builds on the musl artifacts already in
  `out/`; no new code is needed for OHOS once a kernel binder is
  available.
- Per `feedback_no_per_app_hacks.md`: every Westlake service / Context /
  Resource / ContentResolver is package-agnostic. No noice-specific or
  MCD-specific branches anywhere in `shim/java/com/westlake/services/*`.
  Discovery harnesses (`NoiceDiscoverWrapper.java`) are app-specific by
  necessity; the under-test artifacts are not.
- DOC1 (this audit) renumbered `M4_DISCOVERY.md` from 26+1-duplicate
  sections to 28 sequential sections. The duplicate was §15 (M4-power
  written first, then M4a inserted with the same number); M4a moved to
  §17. All downstream sections shifted +1; the M4d+M4e batch (originally
  written as `## §28`) is now `## 28.` Cross-references inside the
  doc were also shifted where appropriate; see
  `M4_DISCOVERY_RENUMBER_NOTES.md` for the audit log.
